GT: -c0*A**c1 + c2*_t*sin(log(A + c3))
Candidate formulas: 62

GT is the fixed function (independent of `t`):
\[
f(A)= -0.17495597007573369\,A^2 + 0.59132419335575606\;\sin(\log(A+1)).
\]
So any matching candidate must (i) have an \(A^2\) polynomial term with the correct coefficient, (ii) have a \(\sin(\log(A+1))\) term with the correct amplitude, and (iii) have **no other nonzero dependence on \(A\)** (no linear \(A\), no rational/exp/log extras), and **no dependence on \(t\)**.

Now check each candidate for whether it can be reduced (by setting its free constants) exactly to \(-kA^2 + m\sin(\log(A+1))\).

4. Rational in \(A\) with \(\log(\exp(A\cdot)+1)\). Not \(\sin(\log(A+1))\). No match.
5. Only logs, no sine-of-log. No match.
6. Logs with Abs/cos/exp inside, no sine-of-log. No match.
7. Form: \(A c0 + c1 + c2\log(Ac3+1) + c4\sin(c5\log(Ac6+1)+c7)\). This has a sine of a log, but it also has an unavoidable \(\log(Ac3+1)\) term unless \(c2=0\), and it has a linear \(A c0\) unless \(c0=0\). Even if set \(c0=0,c2=0\), the remaining term is \(\sin(\alpha\log(\beta A+1)+\gamma)\), which can match \(\sin(\log(A+1))\) by choosing \(\alpha=1,\beta=1,\gamma=0\). I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT:** `-0.17495597*A**2 + 0.59132419*sin(log(A + 1))`

This has two basis functions: `A²` and `sin(log(A+1))`. Note that `_t` is a constant (3.3798...), so `c2*_t = 0.17496 * 3.3798 ≈ 0.59132`.

Let me analyze each candidate systematically. The GT is a sum of:
1. A quadratic term: `-0.175*A²`
2. A sinusoidal term: `0.591*sin(log(A+1))`

I need candidates that can express exactly these two basis functions (and nothing else that can't be zeroed out).

**Key observations:**
- `sin(log(A+1))` is a very specific transcendental function
- Most candidates use `sin(A*c + c)`, `exp(A*c)`, `log(A*c+1)`, rational functions, etc. — these are NOT equivalent to `sin(log(A+1))`
- I need to find candidates containing `sin(log(A+c))` or equivalent

Let me scan for candidates with `sin(log(...))`:

- **Candidate 7**: `A*c0 + c1 + c2*log(A*c3 + 1) + c4*sin(c5*log(A*c6 + 1) + c7)` — Has `sin(c5*log(A*c6+1)+c7)`. Set c0=0, c1=0, c2=0. Then we need `c4*sin(c5*log(A*c6+1)+c7)` to give `-0.175*A² + 0.591*sin(log(A+1))`. But this only gives a sin(log) term, no A² term. **[NO MATCH]**

Wait, let me reconsider. Can `A*c0 + c2*log(A*c3+1)` approximate A²? No, these are different basis functions.

- **Candidate 16**: `c0 + c1*sin(A*c2+c3) + c4*sin(c5*log(c6*exp(c7*Abs(A))+1)+c8)` — The second sin has `log(c6*exp(c7*|A|)+1)`. For A≥0, |A|=A. If c7→0, then `log(c6*1+1)` is constant. This can't produce A². **[NO MATCH]**

- **Candidate 27**: `A²*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(c5*exp(c6*|A|)+1)+c7)` — Has A² term! For A≥0, |A|=A. `log(c5*exp(c6*A)+1)`. If c6→0, `log(c5+1)` = constant. We need `sin(log(A+1))`. Can `c4*log(c5*exp(c6*A)+1)` equal `log(A+1)`? That requires `c5*exp(c6*A)+1 = (A+1)^{c4}`. This doesn't work for general A. **[NO MATCH]**

- **Candidate 20**: `A*c0 + c1 + c2*|A|^c3 + c4*exp(c5*sin(c6*log(c7*|A*c8|+1)+c9))` — For A≥0: has `|A|^c3` (set c3=2 for A²), and `exp(c5*sin(c6*log(c7*A*c8+1)+c9))`. We need `c4*exp(c5*sin(...))` to equal `0.591*sin(log(A+1))`. But exp(sin(...)) ≠ sin(log(...)). **[NO MATCH]**

- **Candidate 50**: `A*c0 + c1 + c2*log(A*c3+1) + c4*sin(c5*log(A*c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)+1)+c9)` — Since t is a variable (not constant in the candidate), but we can set c8=0, making `c7*exp(0)=c7`. Then: `c4*sin(c5*log(A*c6+c7+1)+c9)`. Set c0=0, c1=0, c2=0, c5=1, c9=0, c6=1, c7=0: `c4*sin(log(A+1))`. But no A² term available (only A*c0, log terms). **[NO MATCH]**
